============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (PO12)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - beta*Abs(v)**c1 - omega0**c2*(gamma*t + c3)*x - omega0**c4*x
Candidate formulas: 50

GT (fixed function):
\[
0.415528810853583\sin t\;-\;0.0493727442837992\,v^3\;-\;0.291667748408705\,|v|^{1/3}\;-\;1.02930087898757\,x(0.0222734330694684\,t+1)\;-\;1.02930087898757\,x
\]
Combine the two \(x\) terms:
\[
=0.4155\sin t\;-\;0.04937\,v^3\;-\;0.29167\,|v|^{1/3}\;-\;(1.02930087898757\cdot 0.0222734330694684)\,t x\;-\;(2.05860175797514)\,x
\]
So GT is exactly of the form:
- sinusoid in \(t\) only,
- \(v^3\),
- \(|v|^{1/3}\),
- \(t x\),
- \(x\),
- **no constant offset**, and **no other \(v\)-dependence** (no \(|v|\), no rational \((|v|+1)^{-2}\), no exp/log/cos of \(v\), etc.).

Also \(\sin t\) can be represented as \(\cos(t+\phi)\) by choosing \(\phi=-\pi/2\).

Now check candidates.

### Candidates 1–2
1 has \(\cos(c1+t)\) (ok for \(\sin t\)), has \(v^3\) (ok), has \(v^{c3}\) (can set \(c3=3\) but then duplicates \(v^3\); or set \(c2=0\)), has \(t x\) and \(x\) (ok), **but** the only absolute-value power term is \(c7|v|\) and \(c6/(|v|+1)^2\). There is **no way** to produce \(|v|^{1/3}\) from \(|v|\) or \((|v|+1)^{-2}\) by parameter choice. So cannot match.
2 similarly has \(v^{c5}\) and \(v^3\) and \(t x\), \(x\), \(|v|\), \((|v|+1)^{-2}\), but no \(|v|^{1/3}\). Cannot match.

### Candidates 3, 9, 19–21, 25–26
These replace the needed \(|v|^{1/3}\) with various cosine/log/cos-of-\(|v|\) constructions plus \((|v|+1)^{-2}\). None can equal a pure power \(|v|^{1/3}\) for all real \(v\) by choosing constants (they are bounded/oscillatory or rational/log forms). Also they still lack a direct \(|v|^{1/3}\) term. Cannot match.

### Candidates 4–8, 11–12, 14–15, 17–18, 28, 31–32
All of these are variants of:
\[
\cos(t+\cdot)+ v^{c3} + v^3 + t x + (|v|+1)^{-2} + |v| + \text{(constant)} + x
\]
They **do not contain** \(|v|^{1/3}\). The only absolute-value dependence is linear \(|v|\) (and sometimes the rational term). No parameter choice converts linear \(|v|\) into \(|v|^{1/3}\) globally. So cannot match.

### Candidates 10, 13, 16, 22–24, 29–30
- 10 has \(v^3\) and \(v^{c6}\) (could set \(c6=1/3\) but that gives \(v^{1/3}\), **not** \(|v|^{1/3}\); for negative \(v\), \(v^{1/3}\neq |v|^{1/3}\) (it’s negative vs positive). Domain is sign-changing, so not equivalent. Also it has \(c8|v|\) not \(|v|^{1/3}\).
- 13 has \(v^{c5}\) (again would be \(v^{1/3}\), not \(|v|^{1/3}\)) plus \(|v|\) terms; no \(|v|^{1/3}\).
- 16 has \(|v|\) and an extra \(+|v|\) but still no \(|v|^{1/3}\).
- 22 introduces \(\sin(c3 v+c4)\) (oscillatory in \(v\)), not a power \(|v|^{1/3}\).
- 23 has two free \(v\)-powers \(v^{c5}\) and \(v^{c8}\) but both are powers of \(v\), not \(|v|\); cannot reproduce \(|v|^{1/3}\) on sign-changing domain.
- 24 has \((c3|v|+1)^2\) (quadratic in \(|v|\)), not \(|v|^{1/3}\).
- 29–30 similarly only allow \(v^{c5}\) (power of \(v\), not \(|v|\)) plus \(v^3\), and possibly \((|v|+1)^{-2}\). Cannot match.

### Candidates 27, 33–50
These introduce extra non-GT structures: \((c9+v)^{-3}\), exp terms, \(v/(|v|+1)\), \(v|v|\), Max(0,-v), etc. To match GT exactly, all such extra terms must be set to zero via coefficients. Even if we zero them out, we still face the core issue: none of these candidates contains a \(|v|^{1/3}\) term. Some have \(v|v|\) (i.e., \(|v|v\)), which is \(\pm v^2\), not \(|v|^{1/3}\). Some have only \(v^{c}\) (power of \(v\)), which cannot equal \(|v|^{1/3}\) for negative \(v\). Therefore cannot match.

### Trig phase-shift check
Where candidates have \(\cos(c+t)\), we *can* match \(0.4155\sin t\) by choosing amplitude and phase appropriately. This part is not the blocker.

### Final blocker (common to all candidates)
GT requires an explicit \(-0.2916677\,|v|^{1/3}\) term. No candidate includes \(|v|^{c}\) with a free exponent; they include at best \(|v|\), rational functions of \(|v|\), or powers of \(v\) (not absolute). Because \(v\) can be negative, \(v^{1/3}\) is not equal to \(|v|^{1/3}\) globally, so candidates with \(v^{c}\) cannot substitute for the GT’s \(|v|^{1/3}\).

Therefore no candidate can be made identical to the GT for all real \(x,t,v\).

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match
============================================================

GT Equivalence Verification (PO12)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - beta*Abs(v)**c1 - omega0**c2*(gamma*t + c3)*x - omega0**c4*x
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.0493727*v³ - 1.02930*(0.02227*t + 1)*x - 1.02930*x + 0.41553*sin(t) - 0.29167*|v|^(1/3)`

Let me simplify the GT:
- `sin(t)` term: `0.41553*sin(t)`
- `v³` term: `-0.0493727*v³`
- `x` terms: `-1.02930*(0.02227*t + 1)*x - 1.02930*x = -1.02930*0.02227*t*x - 1.02930*x - 1.02930*x = -0.02293*t*x - 2.05860*x`
- `|v|^(1/3)` term: `-0.29167*|v|^(1/3)`

So GT = `0.41553*sin(t) - 0.0493727*v³ - 2.05860*x - 0.02293*t*x - 0.29167*|v|^(1/3)`

The GT has these basis functions:
1. `sin(t)` (equivalently `cos(t + phase)`)
2. `v³`
3. `x`
4. `t*x`
5. `|v|^(1/3)`

No constant offset term (or it's zero).

Now I need to check each candidate. The key question for each is whether it can represent `|v|^(1/3)` (a fractional power of |v|).

**Candidates with `v**c` terms (where c can be set to 1/3):** These can potentially match.

**Candidates with `1/(|v|+1)²`, `exp(c*v)`, `log(...)`, `cos(...)` of v, etc.:** These CANNOT exactly equal `|v|^(1/3)` — they are fundamentally different basis functions.

Let me categorize:

**Candidates with `v**c` AND no extra non-eliminable terms:**

For a candidate to match, it needs:
- `cos(c+t)` or `sin(t)` ✓
- `v³` ✓
- `x` ✓
- `t*x` ✓
- `v**c` (with c freely choosable = 1/3) ✓
- No extra terms that can't be zeroed out
- No constant term (or a free constant that can be set to 0)

Let me check candidates with `v**c` terms and without problematic extra basis functions:

**Candidate 10:** `c0*x + c1 + c2*cos(c3+t) + c4*v³ + c5*v**c6 + c7*t*x + c8*|v|`

Has `|v|` term that can't be zeroed (c8 can be set to 0). Wait, c8 IS free, so set c8=0. Then: `c0*x + c1 + c2*cos(c3+t) + c4*v³ + c5*v**c6 + c7*t*x`. Set c1=0, c6=1/3. This gives all needed terms. ✓

But wait - GT has `|v|^(1/3)`, and `v**c6` with c6=1/3 gives `v^(1/3)`, not `|v|^(1/3)`. Since v takes both signs, `v^(1/3)` is an odd function while `|v|^(1/3)` is an even function. These are NOT the same. This is a critical distinction.

So I need candidates that have `|v|^c` or `Abs(v)**c`, not just `v**c`.

Looking back at the GT: it has `-beta*Abs(v)**c1` where c1=1/3. So I need `Abs(v)**c` in candidates.

**Candidate 13:** `c0*x + c1 + c2*cos(c3+t) + c4*v**c5 + c6*v³ + c7*t*x + c8*|v| + c9*|v|`

Has `v**c5` (not `|v|**c5`), and `|v|` terms. The `|v|` terms combine to `(c8+c9)*|v|`. But `|v|` ≠ `|v|^(1/3)`. And `v**c5` with c5=1/3 gives odd function. **NO MATCH**

Let me re-examine: Actually, in many symbolic regression frameworks, `v**c` for fractional c might implicitly mean `|v|**c` or handle sign. But strictly mathematically, `v^(1/3)` is odd (real cube root) while `|v|^(1/3)` is even.

Given the domain constraints state v takes both signs, this distinction matters critically.

Looking through ALL candidates, NONE have `Abs(v)**c` as a term — they have either `v**c` or `Abs(v)` (power 1) or `1/(Abs(v)+1)²`. None can produce `|v|^(1/3)`.

Therefore, no candidate can exactly match the GT.
